## The filter
### 1) Feature inventory
In your world, a â€œfeatureâ€ is not a worksheet or module. It is a **concrete mechanism component** that exists whether or not the prospect uses it perfectly.

Examples of your real features:
- Predictive rule exposure (Natural Loop)
- Signal separation under load (MOSAEIC)
- Protective prediction surfacing (Replay Loop Breaker)
- Belief mismatch testing (Conviction Gauntlet)
- External initiation cue (Execution Engine)
- Relational anchoring (Growth Anchor)

If it is not concrete, it is not a feature. It is a claim.

### 2) Why each feature exists
This is where you answer: â€œWhy does this exist for this avatar specifically?â€

Example:
- External initiation cues exist because high load makes internal decision-making unreliable.
- Signal separation exists because fused urgency feels like truth.

This is the â€œreason whyâ€ foundation that keeps you from writing faux benefits.

### 3) Functional benefit
This is the line youâ€™re already policing hard:
- â€œYou finish what you started even when your system tells you to quit.â€
- â€œYou stay present and respond instead of shutting down.â€

Key rule from the excerpt: functional benefits must be what they would â€œdream about at night.â€ In your market, those are:
- Finish the thing
- Stop the loop quickly
- Stay present under pressure
- Stop disappearing from people
- Stop relapsing into restart cycles

### 4) Dimensionalized benefit
This is your â€œtwo people see the same movieâ€ test.

Your best ones do this:
- Proposal tab switching
- Unexpected feedback on a call
- Dinner career question heat
- Group call fast pace, missing a beat, going quiet

Any experiential that is â€œin the middle of a conversationâ€ fails the chart standard because it does not force a shared picture.

### 5) Emotional benefit
Two rules from the excerpt that matter for you:
- Do not tell them what to feel in a generic way.
- Lead them through a scene where the emotion is the only natural outcome.

### What is already aligned

- Your best experiential benefits are hitting the Gene Schwartz standard: specific moment, specific stakes, specific sensory cue.

### Where the filter would tighten you further
